365\t/// Results sorted by name for deterministic output (M5 fix).\n   366\tpub fn list_installed(base_dir: &Path) -> Result<Vec<InstalledLibrary>, JigError> {\n   367\t    let mut libraries = entry.file_name().to_string_lossy().to_string();\n    97\t            let recipe_path = if prefix.is_empty() {\n    98\t                name.clone()\n    99\t            } else {\n   100\t                format!(\"{prefix}/{name}\")\n   101\t            };\n   102\t\n   103\t            // Check if this directory has a recipe.yaml\n   104\t            if path.join(\"recipe.yaml\").exists() {\n   105\t                // Don't shadow library recipes (AC-8.3).\n   106\t                if !library_paths.contains(recipe_path.as_str()) {\n   107\t                    // Try to load description from recipe.\n   108\t                    let desc = Recipe::load(&path.join(\"recipe.yaml\"))\n   109\t                        .ok()\n   110\t                        .and_then(|r| r.description.clone())\n   111\t                        .unwrap_or_else(|| \"(extension)\".to_string());\n   112\t                    entries.push(RecipeEntry {\n   113\t                        path: recipe_path.clone(),\n   114\t                        description: desc,\n   115\t                        source: RecipeSource::Extension,\n   116\t                    });\n   117\t                }\n   118\t            }\n   119\t\n   120\t            // Recurse into subdirectories.\n   121\t            scan_extension_recipes(&path, &recipe_path, library_paths, entries);\n   122\t        }\n   123\t    }\n   124\t}\n   125\t\n   126\t/// Get detailed info about a specific recipe in a library.\n   127\tpub fn recipe_info(\n   128\t    library_name: &str,\n   129\t    recipe_path: &str,\n   130\t    base_dir: &Path,\n   131\t) -> Result<RecipeInfo, JigError> {\n   132\t    let manifest = install::load_installed_manifest(library_name, base_dir)?;\n   133\t\n   134\t    let description = manifest\n   135\t     }\n   178\t    } else {\n   179\t        (Vec::new(), Vec::new())\n   180\t    };\n   181\t\n   182\t    Ok(RecipeInfo {\n   183\t        library: library_name.to_string(),\n   184\t        path: find_undefined_variable(template_source: &str, error_line: Option<usize>, vars: &Value) -> String {\n   180\t    let var_keys: Vec<&str> = match vars.as_object() {\n   181\t        Some(obj) => using Levenshtein distance.\n   216\t/// Looks at all keys in the provided variable context.\n   217\tfn did_you_mean_hint(var_name: &str, vars: &Value) -> String {\n   218\t    let keys: Vec<&str> = parse_position(raw_anchor.position.as_deref(), index, source)?;\n   470\t\n   471\t        Ok(FileOp::Patch {\n   472\t            template,\n   473\t            patch: patch_target,\n   474\t            anchor: Anchor {\n   475\t                pattern: anchor_pattern,\n   476\t                scope,\n   477\t                find: raw_anchor.find,\n   478\t                position,\n   479\t            },\n   480\t            skip_if: raw.skip_if,\n   481\t        })\n   482\t    }\n   483\t}\n   484\t\n   485\t/// Parse and validate injection mode from raw fields.\n   486\tfn parse_inject_mode(\n   487\t    after: &Option<String>,\n   488\t    before: &Option<String>,\n   489\t    prepend: bool,\n   490\t    append: bool,\n   491\t    at: &Option<String>,\n   492\t    index: usize,\n   493\t    source: &Path,\n   494\t) -> Result<InjectMode, JigError> {\n   495\t    let loc = format!(\"files[{index}] in {}\", source.display());\n   496\t\n   497\t    let mode_count = [after.is_some(), before.is_some(), prepend, append]\n   498\t        .iter()\n   499\t        .filter(|&&b| b)\n   500\t        .count();\n   501\t\n   502\t    if mode_count == 0 {\n   503\t        return Err(recipe_err(\n   504\t            \"inject operation missing mode\",\n   505\t            &loc,\n   506\t            \"inject must specify one of: 'after', 'before', 'prepend: true', or 'append: true'\",\n   507\t            \"add an injection mode field\",\n   508\t        ));\n   509\t    }\n   510\t    if mode_count > 1 {\n   511\t        return Err(recipe_err(\n   512\t            \"inject operation has conflicting modes\",\n   513\t            &loc,\n   514\t            \"only one of 'after', 'before', 'prepend', 'append' may be specified\",\n   515\t            \"remove extra injection mode fields so only one remains\",\n   516\t        ));\n   517\t    }\n   518\t\n   519\t    if let Some(pattern) = after {\n   520\t        let pos = parse_match_position(at, index, source)?;\n   521\t        validate_regex(pattern, \"after\", index, source)?;\n   522\t        Ok(InjectMode::After { pattern: pattern.clone(), at: pos })\n   523\t    } else if let Some(pattern) = before {\n   524\t        let pos = parse_match_position(at, index, source)?;\n   525\t        validate_regex(pattern, \"before\", index, source)?;\n   526\t        Ok(InjectMode::Before { pattern: pattern.clone(), at: pos })\n   527\t    } else if prepend {\n   528\t        Ok(InjectMode::Prepend)\n   529\t    } else {\n   530\t        Ok(InjectMode::Append)\n   531\t    }\n   532\t}\n   533\t\n   534\tfn parse_match_position(\n   535\t    at: &Option<String>,\n   536\t    _index: usize,\n   537\t    _source: &Path,\n   538\t) -> Result<MatchPosition, JigError> {\n   539\t    match at.as_deref() {\n   540\t        None | Some(\"first\") => Ok(MatchPosition::First),\n   541\t        Some(\"last\") => Ok(MatchPosition::Last),\n   542\t        Some(other) => Err(recipe_err(\n   543\t            &format!(\"invalid 'at' value: '{other}'\"),\n   544\t            &format!(\"files[{_index}] in {}\", _source.display()),\n   545\t            \"at must be 'first' or 'last'\",\n   546\t            \"use at: first or at: last\",\n   547\t        )),\n   548\t    }\n   549\t}\n   550\t\n   551\tfn validate_regex(pattern: &str, field: &str, index: usize, source: &Path) -> Result<(), JigError> {\n   552\t    if pattern.is_empty() {\n   553\t        return Err(recipe_err(\n   554\t            &format!(\"empty regex pattern in '{field}' field\"),\n   555\t            &format!(\"files[{index}] in {}\", source.display()),\n   556\t            \"an empty pattern matches every line, which is almost certainly not intended\",\n   557\t            \"provide a non-empty regex pattern\",\n   558\t        ));\n   559\t    }\n   560\t    regex::Regex::new(pattern).map_err(|e| recipe_err(\n   561\t        &format!(\"invalid regex in '{field}' field\"),\n   562\t        &format!(\"files[{index}] in {}\", source.display()),\n   563\t        &format!(\"pattern '{pattern}' failed to compile: {e}\"),\n   564\t        \"check regex syntax — remember to escape special characters\",\n   565\t    ))?;\n   566\t    Ok(())\n   567\t}\n   568\t\n   569\tfn parse_fallback(value: Option<&str>, index: usize, source: &Path) -> Result<Fallback, JigError> {\n   570\t    match &Path,\n   147\t    work_dir: &Path,\n   148\t    current: &Path,\n   149\t    diffs: &mut Vec<(String, String)>,\n   150\t) {\n   151\t    for entry in fs::read_dir(current).unwrap() {\n   152\t 202\t            }\n   203\t        }\n   204\t        (serde_json::Value::Array(exp_arr), serde_json::Value::Array(act_arr)) => {\n   205\t            assert_eq!(\n   206\t
